<html><head></head><body style="overflow-wrap: break-word; -webkit-nbsp-mode: space; line-break: after-white-space;"><div># fracttalix_sentinel_v900.py</div><div># Fracttalix Sentinel v9.0 — Three-Channel Extension</div><div>#</div><div># V9.0 extends the v8.0 detection architecture to implement the</div><div># three-channel model of dissipative network information transmission</div><div># derived in the Meta-Kaizen Paper 6 theoretical framework.</div><div>#</div><div># Three-channel model:</div><div># &nbsp; Channel 1 (Structural): Network topology as active transmitter.</div><div># &nbsp; &nbsp; V9.0 monitors structural properties of the input data stream</div><div># &nbsp; &nbsp; as an independent information channel.</div><div>#</div><div># &nbsp; Channel 2 (Rhythmic): Broadband multiplexed oscillatory transmission.</div><div># &nbsp; &nbsp; V9.0 decomposes the composite rhythmicity signal into independent</div><div># &nbsp; &nbsp; frequency band carrier waves and monitors cross-frequency coupling</div><div># &nbsp; &nbsp; between bands as a higher-order information channel.</div><div>#</div><div># &nbsp; Channel 3 (Temporal): One-way irreversible carrier wave.</div><div># &nbsp; &nbsp; V9.0 logs the temporal sequence of channel degradation events</div><div># &nbsp; &nbsp; as diagnostic information about regime change type and severity.</div><div>#</div><div># New alert classes:</div><div># &nbsp; BAND_ANOMALY: Per-carrier-wave anomaly invisible to composite detection</div><div># &nbsp; COUPLING_DEGRADATION: Cross-frequency coupling breakdown (earlier warning)</div><div># &nbsp; STRUCTURAL_RHYTHMIC_DECOUPLING: Channel 1-2 coherence loss</div><div># &nbsp; CASCADE_PRECURSOR: Tipping cascade precursor — CRITICAL severity</div><div>#</div><div># V8.0 root-cause fixes (α-ε) preserved:</div><div># &nbsp; α: SentinelConfig frozen dataclass — immutable, picklable, inspectable</div><div># &nbsp; β: WindowBank — named independent deques; each consumer owns its window slot</div><div># &nbsp; γ: Pipeline decomposition — 26 DetectorStep subclasses (19 v8 + 7 new v9)</div><div># &nbsp; δ: Soft regime boost (T0-02) — replaces hard alpha reset with multiplicative boost</div><div># &nbsp; ε: SSI replaces RSI naming (T0-05); rsi alias preserved</div><div>#</div><div># Governing principle: The v8.0 19-step pipeline is the foundation.</div><div># V9.0 extends it. No existing step is removed. No existing behavior changed.</div><div># All extensions are additive. Full backward compatibility with v8.0 and v7.x.</div><div>#</div><div># Theoretical foundation: Fractal Rhythm Model Papers 1-6</div><div># DOI: 10.5281/zenodo.18859299</div><div># GitHub: https://github.com/thomasbrennan/Fracttalix</div><div><br></div><div>__version__ = "9.0.0"</div><div>__author__ = "Thomas Brennan &amp; Claude (Anthropic) &amp; Grok (xAI)"</div><div>__license__ = "CC0"</div><div><br></div><div>__all__ = [</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; "SentinelConfig", "WindowBank", "StepContext", "DetectorStep",</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; "SentinelDetector", "SentinelResult", "MultiStreamSentinel",</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; "SentinelBenchmark", "SentinelServer",</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; "Detector_7_10", "register_step",</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # V9.0 data structures</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; "FrequencyBands", "StructuralSnapshot", "CouplingMatrix",</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; "ChannelCoherence", "DegradationSequence",</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; "AlertSeverity", "AlertType", "Alert",</div><div>]</div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># Standard library imports</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>import abc</div><div>import argparse</div><div>import asyncio</div><div>import csv</div><div>import dataclasses</div><div>import io</div><div>import json</div><div>import math</div><div>import os</div><div>import socket</div><div>import sys</div><div>import threading</div><div>import time</div><div>import warnings</div><div>from collections import deque</div><div>from enum import Enum</div><div>from typing import Any, Callable, Dict, List, Optional, Sequence, Tuple, Union</div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># Optional third-party imports</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; import numpy as np</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; _NP = True</div><div>except ImportError:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; np = None &nbsp;# type: ignore</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; _NP = False</div><div><br></div><div>try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; from numba import njit as _numba_njit</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; _NUMBA = True</div><div>except ImportError:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _numba_njit(*a, **kw): &nbsp;# type: ignore</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; def _d(f): return f</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return _d</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; _NUMBA = False</div><div><br></div><div>try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; import matplotlib.pyplot as plt</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; import matplotlib.patches as mpatches</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; _MPL = True</div><div>except ImportError:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; plt = None &nbsp;# type: ignore</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; _MPL = False</div><div><br></div><div>try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; from tqdm import tqdm as _tqdm</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; _TQDM = True</div><div>except ImportError:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _tqdm(it, *a, **kw): return it &nbsp;# type: ignore</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; _TQDM = False</div><div><br></div><div>import multiprocessing as _mp</div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># Module-level helpers (must be top-level for pickle / multiprocessing safety)</div><div># T0-03: lambda replaced with named functions</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>def _mean(seq):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Plain-Python mean — pickle-safe (T0-03)."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; s = list(seq)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; return sum(s) / len(s) if s else 0.0</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>def _phase_randomize_worker(args):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Pool worker for phase-randomization surrogates (T0-03)."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; data, seed = args</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; rng = _np_rng(seed)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; arr = _to_np(data)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; fft = _np_fft(arr)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; phases = rng.uniform(0, 2 * math.pi, len(fft) // 2 + 1)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; fft_r = fft.copy()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(fft_r)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; for i in range(1, n // 2 + 1):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fft_r[i] *= math.cos(phases[i - 1]) + 1j * math.sin(phases[i - 1])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if n - i != i:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fft_r[n - i] = fft_r[i].conjugate()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; return _np_ifft(fft_r).real.tolist()</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>def _np_rng(seed=None):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return np.random.default_rng(seed)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; import random</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; class _R:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, s): random.seed(s)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; def uniform(self, lo, hi, n): return [random.uniform(lo, hi) for _ in range(n)]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; return _R(seed)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>def _to_np(data):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return np.asarray(data, dtype=float)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; return list(data)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>def _np_fft(arr):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return np.fft.rfft(arr)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(arr)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; return [complex(arr[k]) for k in range(n)] &nbsp;# stub</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>def _np_ifft(arr):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return np.fft.irfft(arr)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; return arr &nbsp;# stub</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># V9.0 DATA STRUCTURES — Three-Channel Model</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>@dataclasses.dataclass(frozen=True)</div><div>class FrequencyBands:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Channel 2 decomposition into five independent carrier waves.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Computed via FFT decomposition of windowed signal.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Five bands: ultra-low (trend), low (slow oscillation),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; mid (primary rhythmicity), high (fast fluctuation),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ultra-high (noise floor).</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ultra_low_power: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; low_power: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; mid_power: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; high_power: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ultra_high_power: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ultra_low_phase: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; low_phase: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; mid_phase: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; high_phase: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ultra_high_phase: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; timestamp: int</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>@dataclasses.dataclass(frozen=True)</div><div>class StructuralSnapshot:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Channel 1 structural properties at current timestep.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Treats network topology as active transmitter — not passive substrate.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Encodes history, identity, and capacity of the input data stream</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; at the current moment independently of rhythmic properties.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; mean: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; variance: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; skewness: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; kurtosis: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; autocorrelation_lag1: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; autocorrelation_lag2: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; stationarity_score: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; timestamp: int</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>@dataclasses.dataclass(frozen=True)</div><div>class CouplingMatrix:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Cross-frequency coupling coefficients between adjacent band pairs.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Phase-amplitude coupling: lower band phase to higher band amplitude.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Coupling degradation is an earlier warning signal than single-band</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; anomaly — the heterodyned information channel degrades first.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Declining composite_coupling_score precedes regime change.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ultra_low_to_low: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; low_to_mid: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; mid_to_high: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; high_to_ultra_high: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; composite_coupling_score: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; coupling_trend: float &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Positive = strengthening, negative = degrading</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; timestamp: int</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>@dataclasses.dataclass(frozen=True)</div><div>class ChannelCoherence:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Structural-rhythmic coherence measurement.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Measures degree to which Channel 1 and Channel 2 remain coupled.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; In a healthy network structural changes are reflected in rhythmic</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; changes and vice versa. Decoupling indicates channels have lost</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; coherence — itself a regime change signal independent of anomalies</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; in either individual channel.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; coherence_score: 0.0 = fully decoupled, 1.0 = fully coherent.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; coherence_score: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; structural_change_rate: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; rhythmic_change_rate: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; decoupling_trend: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; timestamp: int</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>@dataclasses.dataclass(frozen=True)</div><div>class DegradationSequence:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Temporal ordering of channel degradation events (Channel 3 information).</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; The sequence and ordering of degradation is diagnostic about regime</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; change type and severity.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; first_channel_anomaly: str</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; first_anomaly_timestamp: int</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; second_channel_anomaly: Optional[str]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; second_anomaly_timestamp: Optional[int]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; coupling_degradation_timestamp: Optional[int]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; decoupling_timestamp: Optional[int]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; cascade_precursor_timestamp: Optional[int]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; sequence_pattern: str &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Human-readable degradation narrative</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>class AlertSeverity(Enum):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Severity levels for v9.0 structured alerts."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; INFO = 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; WARNING = 2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ALERT = 3</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; CRITICAL = 4 &nbsp; &nbsp;# Reserved for CASCADE_PRECURSOR only</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>class AlertType(Enum):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Alert type classification for v9.0 structured alerts."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # v8.0 alert type identifiers (as string labels)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; POINT_ANOMALY = "point_anomaly"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; CONTEXTUAL_ANOMALY = "contextual_anomaly"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; COLLECTIVE_ANOMALY = "collective_anomaly"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; DRIFT_ANOMALY = "drift_anomaly"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; VARIANCE_ANOMALY = "variance_anomaly"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; REGIME_CHANGE = "regime_change"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; EWS_WARNING = "ews_warning"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # V9.0 alert types</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; BAND_ANOMALY = "band_anomaly"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; COUPLING_DEGRADATION = "coupling_degradation"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; STRUCTURAL_RHYTHMIC_DECOUPLING = "sr_decoupling"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; CASCADE_PRECURSOR = "cascade_precursor"</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>@dataclasses.dataclass(frozen=True)</div><div>class Alert:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Structured alert object for v9.0 three-channel detection."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; alert_type: AlertType</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; severity: AlertSeverity</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; score: float</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; message: str</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>def _build_sequence_narrative(alert_types_set: set) -&gt; str:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Build human-readable degradation narrative from active alert type set."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parts = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if AlertType.BAND_ANOMALY in alert_types_set:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parts.append("carrier wave anomaly detected")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if AlertType.COUPLING_DEGRADATION in alert_types_set:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parts.append("cross-frequency coupling degrading")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if AlertType.STRUCTURAL_RHYTHMIC_DECOUPLING in alert_types_set:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parts.append("structural-rhythmic channels decoupling")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if AlertType.CASCADE_PRECURSOR in alert_types_set:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parts.append("CASCADE PRECURSOR — scale-level reversion risk")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if not parts:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parts.append("no active degradation")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; return " \u2192 ".join(parts)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># SECTION 1 — SentinelConfig (frozen dataclass, α)</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div>@dataclasses.dataclass(frozen=True, slots=True)</div><div>class SentinelConfig:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Immutable configuration for SentinelDetector.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; All parameters validated in ``__post_init__``. &nbsp;Use the factory class</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; methods (``fast``, ``production``, ``sensitive``, ``realtime``) for</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; common presets, or override individual fields via ``dataclasses.replace``.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # A: Core EWMA</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; alpha: float = 0.1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """EWMA smoothing factor (0 &lt; α ≤ 1). &nbsp;Smaller = slower, more stable."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; dev_alpha: float = 0.1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """EWMA factor for deviation (volatility) estimation."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; multiplier: float = 3.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Alert threshold = EWMA ± multiplier × dev_ewma."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; warmup_periods: int = 30</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Observations collected before alerts are issued."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # B: Regime detection</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; regime_threshold: float = 3.5</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Z-score magnitude that triggers a regime change."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; regime_alpha_boost: float = 2.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Multiplicative boost applied to alpha during regime transitions (δ)."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; regime_boost_decay: float = 0.9</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Decay rate of the regime boost per observation."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # C: Multivariate</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; multivariate: bool = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Enable multivariate (Mahalanobis) mode."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; n_channels: int = 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Number of input channels when multivariate=True."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; cov_alpha: float = 0.05</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """EWMA factor for covariance matrix update."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # D: FRM metrics</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; rpi_window: int = 64</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Window length for RPI FFT computation."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; rfi_window: int = 64</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Window length for RFI inter-beat analysis."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; rpi_threshold: float = 0.6</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Minimum RPI for 'rhythm healthy' classification."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; rfi_threshold: float = 0.4</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """RFI alert threshold (higher = more irregular)."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # E: Complexity &amp; EWS</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; pe_order: int = 3</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Permutation Entropy embedding dimension."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; pe_window: int = 50</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Sliding window for PE computation."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; pe_threshold: float = 0.05</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """PE deviation alert threshold (fraction of log(pe_order!))."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ews_window: int = 40</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """EWS rolling window (T0-01: independent from scalar_window)."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ews_threshold: float = 0.6</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """EWS score threshold for 'approaching critical' classification."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # F: Fluid dynamics</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; sti_window: int = 20</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Shear-Turbulence Index window."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; tps_window: int = 30</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Temporal Phase Space reconstruction window."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; osc_damp_window: int = 20</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Oscillation damping window."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; osc_threshold: float = 1.5</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Oscillation damping alert multiplier."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; cpd_window: int = 30</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Change-Point Detection comparison window."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; cpd_threshold: float = 2.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """CPD alert z-score threshold."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # G: Drift / Volatility / Seasonal</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ph_delta: float = 0.01</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Page-Hinkley incremental delta (sensitivity)."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ph_lambda: float = 50.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Page-Hinkley cumulative threshold."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; var_cusum_k: float = 0.5</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """VarCUSUM allowance (half the expected shift in std-devs)."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; var_cusum_h: float = 5.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """VarCUSUM decision threshold."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; seasonal_period: int = 0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Seasonal period (0 = auto-detect via FFT)."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # H: AQB / Scoring / IO</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; quantile_threshold_mode: bool = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Use Adaptive Quantile Baseline instead of EWMA ± mult threshold."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; aqb_window: int = 200</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Rolling window for AQB quantile estimation."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; aqb_q_low: float = 0.01</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Lower quantile for AQB."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; aqb_q_high: float = 0.99</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Upper quantile for AQB."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; history_maxlen: int = 5000</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Maximum result records kept in memory."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; csv_path: str = ""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """If non-empty, stream results to this CSV file."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; log_level: str = "WARNING"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Python logging level name."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # V9.0 — Channel 2 frequency decomposition</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; enable_frequency_decomposition: bool = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Enable FFT decomposition of signal into five frequency band carrier waves."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; min_window_for_fft: int = 32</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Minimum window length required before FFT decomposition runs."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # V9.0 — Cross-frequency coupling detection</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; enable_coupling_detection: bool = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Enable cross-frequency phase-amplitude coupling measurement."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; coupling_degradation_threshold: float = 0.3</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """composite_coupling_score below this triggers COUPLING_DEGRADATION alert."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; coupling_trend_window: int = 10</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Number of FrequencyBands snapshots used for coupling measurement."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # V9.0 — Structural-rhythmic coherence</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; enable_channel_coherence: bool = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Enable structural-rhythmic channel coherence measurement."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; coherence_threshold: float = 0.4</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """coherence_score below this triggers STRUCTURAL_RHYTHMIC_DECOUPLING alert."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; coherence_window: int = 20</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Rolling window length for coherence computation."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # V9.0 — Cascade precursor</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; enable_cascade_detection: bool = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Enable CASCADE_PRECURSOR detection (requires all three conditions)."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; cascade_ews_threshold: int = 2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Minimum number of EWS indicators elevated for cascade precursor."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # V9.0 — Degradation sequence logging</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; enable_sequence_logging: bool = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Enable temporal logging of channel degradation sequences."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; sequence_retention: int = 1000</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Maximum number of completed degradation sequences to retain."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __post_init__(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; errs = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not (0.0 &lt; self.alpha &lt;= 1.0):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; errs.append(f"alpha={self.alpha} must be in (0, 1]")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not (0.0 &lt; self.dev_alpha &lt;= 1.0):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; errs.append(f"dev_alpha={self.dev_alpha} must be in (0, 1]")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self.multiplier &lt;= 0:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; errs.append(f"multiplier={self.multiplier} must be &gt; 0")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self.warmup_periods &lt; 1:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; errs.append(f"warmup_periods={self.warmup_periods} must be &gt;= 1")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self.n_channels &lt; 1:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; errs.append(f"n_channels={self.n_channels} must be &gt;= 1")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not (0 &lt; self.aqb_q_low &lt; self.aqb_q_high &lt; 1):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; errs.append("aqb_q_low/high must satisfy 0 &lt; low &lt; high &lt; 1")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if errs:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; raise ValueError("SentinelConfig validation errors:\n &nbsp;" + "\n &nbsp;".join(errs))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # Factory presets</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @classmethod</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def fast(cls) -&gt; "SentinelConfig":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """High α, low warmup — react instantly, higher false-positive rate."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return cls(alpha=0.3, dev_alpha=0.3, warmup_periods=10)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @classmethod</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def production(cls) -&gt; "SentinelConfig":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Balanced defaults — suitable for most production deployments."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return cls()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @classmethod</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def sensitive(cls) -&gt; "SentinelConfig":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Low α, tight multiplier — catches subtle anomalies."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return cls(alpha=0.05, dev_alpha=0.05, multiplier=2.5, warmup_periods=50)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @classmethod</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def realtime(cls) -&gt; "SentinelConfig":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Fast response with quantile-adaptive thresholds."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return cls(alpha=0.2, warmup_periods=15, quantile_threshold_mode=True)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># SECTION 2 — WindowBank (β)</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div>class WindowBank:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Named collection of independent deques.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Each consumer registers its own slot with its own maxlen; the bank's</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ``append`` method fans out each new value to *all* registered deques.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Slots are independent — one consumer's window size does not affect others.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; T0-01 fix: EWSStep registers ``"ews_w"`` independently of ``"scalar"``</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; so it never receives stale scalar_window data.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._windows: Dict[str, deque] = {}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def register(self, name: str, maxlen: int) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Create a named window. &nbsp;No-op if already registered."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if name not in self._windows:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._windows[name] = deque(maxlen=maxlen)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def append(self, value: float) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Fan out *value* to every registered window."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for d in self._windows.values():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; d.append(value)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def get(self, name: str) -&gt; deque:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Return the named deque (raises KeyError if not registered)."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self._windows[name]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Clear all windows, preserving registrations."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for d in self._windows.values():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; d.clear()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, list]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {k: list(v) for k, v in self._windows.items()}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, list]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for k, vals in sd.items():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if k in self._windows:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._windows[k].clear()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._windows[k].extend(vals)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># SECTION 3 — StepContext</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div>@dataclasses.dataclass</div><div>class StepContext:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Mutable scratchpad passed through the pipeline on each observation.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Steps read previous results from ``scratch`` and write their own outputs</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; into it. &nbsp;``value`` is the raw input; ``step`` is the observation counter.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; value: Any</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Raw input value (scalar float or list/array for multivariate)."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; step: int</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Monotonically increasing observation counter (0-based)."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; config: SentinelConfig</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Immutable detector configuration."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; bank: WindowBank</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Shared window bank."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; scratch: Dict[str, Any] = dataclasses.field(default_factory=dict)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Shared mutable scratchpad — steps read/write intermediate results."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # Convenience accessors (populated by CoreEWMAStep)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @property</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def current(self) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Scalar current value (last element if multivariate)."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = self.value</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if isinstance(v, (list, tuple)):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return float(v[-1])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if hasattr(v, '__len__'):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return float(v[-1])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; except Exception:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pass</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return float(v)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @property</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def ewma(self) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self.scratch.get("ewma", 0.0)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @property</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def dev_ewma(self) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self.scratch.get("dev_ewma", 1.0)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @property</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def baseline_mean(self) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self.scratch.get("baseline_mean", 0.0)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @property</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def baseline_std(self) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self.scratch.get("baseline_std", 1.0)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @property</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def is_warmup(self) -&gt; bool:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self.step &lt; self.config.warmup_periods</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># SECTION 4 — DetectorStep ABC + registry</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div>_STEP_REGISTRY: Dict[str, type] = {}</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>def register_step(cls):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Class decorator — register a DetectorStep subclass by name."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; _STEP_REGISTRY[cls.__name__] = cls</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; return cls</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div>class DetectorStep(abc.ABC):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Abstract base for pipeline steps.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Each subclass implements a single well-scoped responsibility. &nbsp;The pipeline</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; calls ``update(ctx)`` in order; steps modify ``ctx.scratch`` in-place.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @abc.abstractmethod</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Process one observation. &nbsp;Modifies ctx.scratch in-place."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @abc.abstractmethod</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Reset internal state to factory defaults."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @abc.abstractmethod</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Return JSON-serialisable snapshot of internal state."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @abc.abstractmethod</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Restore internal state from a snapshot."""</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># SECTION 5 — Pipeline Steps</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.1 CoreEWMAStep</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class CoreEWMAStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Compute EWMA baseline + anomaly score. &nbsp;Must be first in pipeline."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._bank_registered = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ewma = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._dev_ewma = 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._warmup_buf: List[float] = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._initialized = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # per-channel state (multivariate)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_ewma: List[float] = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_dev: List[float] = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_init: List[bool] = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # AQB rolling buffer</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._aqb_buf: deque = deque(maxlen=self.cfg.aqb_window)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # boost state (regime soft-boost injected here by RegimeStep)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._alpha_boost: float = 1.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _ensure_bank(self, bank: WindowBank):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not self._bank_registered:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bank.register("scalar", max(self.cfg.pe_window, self.cfg.rpi_window,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg.rfi_window, self.cfg.sti_window,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg.tps_window, self.cfg.osc_damp_window,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg.cpd_window, 64))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._bank_registered = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _eff_alpha(self) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; a = self.cfg.alpha * self._alpha_boost</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return min(a, 1.0)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _eff_dev_alpha(self) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; a = self.cfg.dev_alpha * self._alpha_boost</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return min(a, 1.0)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _scalar_update(self, v: float, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cfg = self.cfg</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._aqb_buf.append(abs(v - self._ewma) if self._initialized else 0.0)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not self._initialized:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._warmup_buf.append(v)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(self._warmup_buf) &gt;= cfg.warmup_periods:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ewma = _mean(self._warmup_buf)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sq = [(x - self._ewma) ** 2 for x in self._warmup_buf]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._dev_ewma = math.sqrt(_mean(sq)) or 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._initialized = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"ewma": v, "dev_ewma": 1.0, "baseline_mean": v,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "baseline_std": 1.0, "z_score": 0.0,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "anomaly_score": 0.0, "anomaly": False,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "alert": False, "warmup": True}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; a = self._eff_alpha()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; da = self._eff_dev_alpha()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prev_ewma = self._ewma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ewma = a * v + (1 - a) * self._ewma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; err = abs(v - prev_ewma)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._dev_ewma = da * err + (1 - da) * self._dev_ewma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._dev_ewma = max(self._dev_ewma, 1e-10)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; z = (v - self._ewma) / self._dev_ewma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sigma = self.cfg.multiplier</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if cfg.quantile_threshold_mode and len(self._aqb_buf) &gt;= 10:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sorted_buf = sorted(self._aqb_buf)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(sorted_buf)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hi_idx = min(int(cfg.aqb_q_high * n), n - 1)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lo_idx = max(int(cfg.aqb_q_low * n), 0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hi_thresh = self._ewma + sorted_buf[hi_idx]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lo_thresh = self._ewma - sorted_buf[hi_idx]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert = v &gt; hi_thresh or v &lt; lo_thresh</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert = abs(z) &gt; sigma</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; anomaly_score = min(1.0, abs(z) / (sigma + 1e-10))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "ewma": self._ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "dev_ewma": self._dev_ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "baseline_mean": self._ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "baseline_std": self._dev_ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "z_score": z,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "anomaly_score": anomaly_score,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "anomaly": alert,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "alert": alert,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "warmup": False,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _mv_update(self, vs: List[float], ctx: StepContext) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cfg = self.cfg</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; nc = cfg.n_channels</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(self._ch_ewma) &lt; nc:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_ewma = [0.0] * nc</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_dev = [1.0] * nc</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_init = [False] * nc</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; scores = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i, v in enumerate(vs[:nc]):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not self._ch_init[i]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_ewma[i] = v</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_init[i] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; scores.append(0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; a = self._eff_alpha()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; da = self._eff_dev_alpha()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prev = self._ch_ewma[i]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_ewma[i] = a * v + (1 - a) * self._ch_ewma[i]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; err = abs(v - prev)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_dev[i] = da * err + (1 - da) * self._ch_dev[i]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_dev[i] = max(self._ch_dev[i], 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; scores.append(abs(v - self._ch_ewma[i]) / self._ch_dev[i])</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; agg = _mean(scores) if scores else 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; z = agg</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sigma = self.cfg.multiplier</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert = z &gt; sigma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; anomaly_score = min(1.0, z / (sigma + 1e-10))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Use last channel as "scalar" representative</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sv = float(vs[-1]) if vs else 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ewma = self._ch_ewma[-1] if self._ch_ewma else sv</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._dev_ewma = self._ch_dev[-1] if self._ch_dev else 1.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "ewma": self._ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "dev_ewma": self._dev_ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "baseline_mean": self._ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "baseline_std": self._dev_ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "z_score": z,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "anomaly_score": anomaly_score,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "anomaly": alert,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "alert": alert,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "warmup": self._n &lt; self.cfg.warmup_periods,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "ch_ewma": list(self._ch_ewma),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "ch_dev": list(self._ch_dev),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ensure_bank(ctx.bank)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = ctx.value</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cfg = self.cfg</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if cfg.multivariate and isinstance(v, (list, tuple, type(None))):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if v is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = [0.0] * cfg.n_channels</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vals = [float(x) for x in v]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result = self._mv_update(vals, ctx)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sv = float(vals[-1]) if vals else 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sv = float(v)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result = self._scalar_update(sv, ctx)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.bank.append(sv)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch.update(result)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Decay boost</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._alpha_boost = max(1.0, self._alpha_boost * self.cfg.regime_boost_decay)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "ewma": self._ewma, "dev_ewma": self._dev_ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "initialized": self._initialized, "n": self._n,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "warmup_buf": list(self._warmup_buf),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "ch_ewma": list(self._ch_ewma), "ch_dev": list(self._ch_dev),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "ch_init": list(self._ch_init), "alpha_boost": self._alpha_boost,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "aqb_buf": list(self._aqb_buf),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ewma = sd.get("ewma", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._dev_ewma = sd.get("dev_ewma", 1.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._initialized = sd.get("initialized", False)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._warmup_buf = sd.get("warmup_buf", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_ewma = sd.get("ch_ewma", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_dev = sd.get("ch_dev", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ch_init = sd.get("ch_init", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._alpha_boost = sd.get("alpha_boost", 1.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._aqb_buf = deque(sd.get("aqb_buf", []), maxlen=self.cfg.aqb_window)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.2 CUSUMStep</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class CUSUMStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Bidirectional CUSUM for persistent mean shift detection."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_hi = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_lo = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._k = 0.5 &nbsp;# allowance in sigmas</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ctx.is_warmup:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; z = ctx.scratch.get("z_score", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; k = self._k</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_hi = max(0.0, self._s_hi + z - k)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_lo = max(0.0, self._s_lo - z - k)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; h = 5.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cusum_alert = (self._s_hi &gt; h) or (self._s_lo &gt; h)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["cusum_hi"] = self._s_hi</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["cusum_lo"] = self._s_lo</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["cusum_alert"] = cusum_alert</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if cusum_alert:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"s_hi": self._s_hi, "s_lo": self._s_lo}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_hi = sd.get("s_hi", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_lo = sd.get("s_lo", 0.0)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.3 RegimeStep (δ — soft boost, T0-02)</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class RegimeStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Detect regime changes; apply soft alpha boost instead of hard reset (δ)."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._in_regime = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._regime_count = 0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ctx.is_warmup:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["regime_change"] = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; z = abs(ctx.scratch.get("z_score", 0.0))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thresh = self.cfg.regime_threshold</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if z &gt; thresh:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._in_regime = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._regime_count += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Soft boost: tell CoreEWMAStep to temporarily raise alpha (T0-02)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; core = ctx.scratch.get("_core_step_ref")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if core is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; core._alpha_boost = self.cfg.regime_alpha_boost</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["regime_change"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._in_regime:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._in_regime = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["regime_change"] = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["in_regime"] = self._in_regime</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"in_regime": self._in_regime, "regime_count": self._regime_count}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._in_regime = sd.get("in_regime", False)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._regime_count = sd.get("regime_count", 0)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.4 VarCUSUMStep</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class VarCUSUMStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """CUSUM on squared deviation — catches volatility explosions."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_hi = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_lo = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._var_ewma = 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._warmed = False</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ctx.is_warmup:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not self._warmed:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_hi = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_lo = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._var_ewma = 0.0 &nbsp;# seed from real data, not default 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._warmed = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dev = ctx.dev_ewma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; z = ctx.scratch.get("z_score", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v2 = z * z &nbsp;# variance proxy</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._var_ewma = 0.9 * self._var_ewma + 0.1 * v2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; k = self.cfg.var_cusum_k</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_hi = max(0.0, self._s_hi + v2 - k)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Only accumulate _s_lo when variance baseline is established; prevents</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # false "variance drop" alerts on data that has always been constant.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._var_ewma &gt; 1e-4:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_lo = max(0.0, self._s_lo + k - v2)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_lo = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert = self._s_hi &gt; self.cfg.var_cusum_h or self._s_lo &gt; self.cfg.var_cusum_h</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["var_cusum_hi"] = self._s_hi</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["var_cusum_lo"] = self._s_lo</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["var_cusum_alert"] = alert</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if alert:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"s_hi": self._s_hi, "s_lo": self._s_lo, "var_ewma": self._var_ewma, "warmed": self._warmed}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_hi = sd.get("s_hi", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._s_lo = sd.get("s_lo", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._var_ewma = sd.get("var_ewma", 1.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._warmed = sd.get("warmed", False)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.5 PageHinkleyStep</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class PageHinkleyStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Page-Hinkley test for slow gradual mean drift."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cum_hi = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cum_lo = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._m_hi = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._m_lo = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ctx.is_warmup:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ph_alert"] = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = ctx.current</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu = ctx.ewma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; delta = self.cfg.ph_delta</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lam = self.cfg.ph_lambda</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cum_hi += (v - mu - delta)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cum_lo += (mu - v - delta)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._m_hi = max(self._m_hi, self._cum_hi)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._m_lo = max(self._m_lo, self._cum_lo)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert = (self._m_hi - self._cum_hi &gt; lam) or (self._m_lo - self._cum_lo &gt; lam)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ph_alert"] = alert</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ph_cum_hi"] = self._cum_hi</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ph_cum_lo"] = self._cum_lo</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if alert:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # reset to avoid continuous triggering</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cum_hi = 0.0; self._cum_lo = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._m_hi = 0.0; self._m_lo = 0.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"cum_hi": self._cum_hi, "cum_lo": self._cum_lo,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "m_hi": self._m_hi, "m_lo": self._m_lo, "n": self._n}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cum_hi = sd.get("cum_hi", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cum_lo = sd.get("cum_lo", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._m_hi = sd.get("m_hi", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._m_lo = sd.get("m_lo", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.6 STIStep</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class STIStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Shear-Turbulence Index — fluid-dynamics anomaly proxy."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._prev = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._diffs: deque = deque(maxlen=self.cfg.sti_window)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = ctx.current</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._prev is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; d = abs(v - self._prev)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._diffs.append(d)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._prev = v</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(self._diffs) &gt;= 4:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu = _mean(self._diffs)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sq = [(x - mu) ** 2 for x in self._diffs]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; std = math.sqrt(_mean(sq)) or 1e-10</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sti = mu / std if std &gt; 0 else 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sti = 0.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["sti"] = sti</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not ctx.is_warmup and sti &gt; 2.0:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"prev": self._prev, "diffs": list(self._diffs)}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._prev = sd.get("prev")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._diffs = deque(sd.get("diffs", []), maxlen=self.cfg.sti_window)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.7 TPSStep — Temporal Phase Space</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class TPSStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Temporal Phase Space reconstruction — detects attractor deformation."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._win: deque = deque(maxlen=self.cfg.tps_window)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ref_radius: Optional[float] = None</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = ctx.current</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._win.append(v)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(self._win) &lt; self.cfg.tps_window:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["tps_score"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = list(self._win)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu = _mean(w)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Use pairs (x[i], x[i+1]) as 2D phase space</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; radii = [math.sqrt((w[i] - mu) ** 2 + (w[i+1] - mu) ** 2)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;for i in range(len(w) - 1)]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; r_mean = _mean(radii) if radii else 0.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._ref_radius is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ref_radius = r_mean or 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; score = abs(r_mean - self._ref_radius) / (self._ref_radius + 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["tps_score"] = score</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not ctx.is_warmup and score &gt; 0.5:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Slowly update reference</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ref_radius = 0.99 * self._ref_radius + 0.01 * r_mean</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"win": list(self._win), "ref_radius": self._ref_radius}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._win = deque(sd.get("win", []), maxlen=self.cfg.tps_window)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ref_radius = sd.get("ref_radius")</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.8 OscDampStep</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class OscDampStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Oscillation damping — detects sudden amplitude shifts."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._amp_buf: deque = deque(maxlen=self.cfg.osc_damp_window)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._amp_ewma = 0.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = ctx.current</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = ctx.bank.get("scalar")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(w) &gt;= 2:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; amp = max(w) - min(w)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; amp = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._amp_buf.append(amp)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alpha = 0.1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._amp_ewma = alpha * amp + (1 - alpha) * self._amp_ewma</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not ctx.is_warmup and self._amp_ewma &gt; 1e-10:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ratio = amp / self._amp_ewma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; osc_alert = ratio &gt; self.cfg.osc_threshold or ratio &lt; (1.0 / self.cfg.osc_threshold)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; osc_alert = False</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["osc_amp"] = amp</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["osc_alert"] = osc_alert</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if osc_alert:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"amp_buf": list(self._amp_buf), "amp_ewma": self._amp_ewma}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._amp_buf = deque(sd.get("amp_buf", []), maxlen=self.cfg.osc_damp_window)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._amp_ewma = sd.get("amp_ewma", 0.0)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.9 CPDStep — Change Point Detection</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class CPDStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Two-window CPD: compare means of recent vs historical windows."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._hist: deque = deque(maxlen=self.cfg.cpd_window * 2)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = ctx.current</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._hist.append(v)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = self.cfg.cpd_window</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(self._hist) &lt; w * 2 or ctx.is_warmup:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["cpd_score"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; h = list(self._hist)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; recent = h[-w:]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; historical = h[:w]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu_r = _mean(recent)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu_h = _mean(historical)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sq_h = [(x - mu_h) ** 2 for x in historical]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; std_h = math.sqrt(_mean(sq_h)) if sq_h else 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; std_h = max(std_h, 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; score = abs(mu_r - mu_h) / std_h</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["cpd_score"] = score</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if score &gt; self.cfg.cpd_threshold:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"hist": list(self._hist)}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._hist = deque(sd.get("hist", []), maxlen=self.cfg.cpd_window * 2)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.10 RPIStep — Rhythm Periodicity Index (FRM Axiom 6)</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class RPIStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """RPI via FFT dominant peak ratio."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = ctx.bank.get("scalar")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(w) &lt; self.cfg.rpi_window or not _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["rpi"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; arr = np.array(list(w)[-self.cfg.rpi_window:])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; arr = arr - arr.mean()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; spec = np.abs(np.fft.rfft(arr)) ** 2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; total = spec.sum()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if total &lt; 1e-12:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["rpi"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rpi = float(spec.max() / total)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["rpi"] = rpi</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not ctx.is_warmup and rpi &lt; self.cfg.rpi_threshold:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pass &nbsp;# low RPI is informational, not an alert by itself</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"n": self._n}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.11 RFIStep — Rhythm Fractal Index (FRM Axiom 8)</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class RFIStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """RFI: Hurst-like fractal dimension of rhythm irregularity."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _hurst(self, ts: List[float]) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(ts)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if n &lt; 8:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.5</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu = _mean(ts)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dev = [x - mu for x in ts]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # R/S analysis</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumdev = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; s = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for d in dev:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; s += d</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumdev.append(s)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; R = max(cumdev) - min(cumdev)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sq = [(x - mu) ** 2 for x in ts]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; S = math.sqrt(_mean(sq)) or 1e-10</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rs = R / S</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if rs &lt;= 0:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.5</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return math.log(rs) / math.log(n / 2) if n &gt; 2 else 0.5</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = ctx.bank.get("scalar")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(w) &lt; self.cfg.rfi_window:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["rfi"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["hurst"] = 0.5</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ts = list(w)[-self.cfg.rfi_window:]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; h = self._hurst(ts)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rfi = abs(h - 0.5) * 2 &nbsp;# 0=random, 1=perfectly fractal</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["rfi"] = rfi</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["hurst"] = h</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not ctx.is_warmup and rfi &gt; self.cfg.rfi_threshold:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"n": self._n}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp;
