&nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.12 SSIStep — Synchrony Stability Index (FRM Axiom 10) — was RSI (T0-05)</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class SSIStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """SSI: Kuramoto synchronization proxy via FFT phase coherence.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Formerly mislabeled 'RSI' in v7.10 (T0-05 fix). &nbsp;``rsi`` attribute alias</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; preserved for backward compatibility.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = ctx.bank.get("scalar")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = self.cfg.rpi_window</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(w) &lt; n or not _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ssi"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["rsi"] = 0.0 &nbsp;# alias (T0-05)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; arr = np.array(list(w)[-n:])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; arr = arr - arr.mean()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fft = np.fft.rfft(arr)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; phases = np.angle(fft[1:]) &nbsp;# skip DC</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Kuramoto order param: |mean(exp(i*phases))|</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; order = float(np.abs(np.mean(np.exp(1j * phases))))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ssi"] = order</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["rsi"] = order &nbsp;# backward compat alias</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"n": self._n}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.13 PEStep — Permutation Entropy (FRM Axiom 3)</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class PEStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Streaming Permutation Entropy."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _ordinal_pattern(self, window: List[float]) -&gt; tuple:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return tuple(sorted(range(len(window)), key=lambda i: window[i]))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _pe(self, data: List[float], m: int) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; from math import log, factorial</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(data)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; counts: Dict[tuple, int] = {}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; total = 0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in range(n - m + 1):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pat = self._ordinal_pattern(data[i:i+m])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; counts[pat] = counts.get(pat, 0) + 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; total += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if total == 0:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; h = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for c in counts.values():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; p = c / total</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if p &gt; 0:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; h -= p * math.log(p)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; max_h = math.log(math.factorial(m)) if m &gt; 1 else 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return h / max_h if max_h &gt; 0 else 0.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pe_ewma = 0.5</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = ctx.bank.get("scalar")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; m = self.cfg.pe_order</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(w) &lt; max(self.cfg.pe_window, m + 1):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["pe"] = 0.5</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["pe_baseline"] = self._pe_ewma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; data = list(w)[-self.cfg.pe_window:]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pe = self._pe(data, m)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["pe"] = pe</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Rolling PE baseline</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alpha = 0.05</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pe_ewma = alpha * pe + (1 - alpha) * self._pe_ewma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["pe_baseline"] = self._pe_ewma</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Alert on contextual deviation (not absolute low PE — fixes v7.11 false alarm)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dev = abs(pe - self._pe_ewma)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not ctx.is_warmup and dev &gt; self.cfg.pe_threshold:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"pe_ewma": self._pe_ewma, "n": self._n}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pe_ewma = sd.get("pe_ewma", 0.5)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.14 EWSStep — Early Warning Signals (FRM Axiom 9) — T0-01 fix</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class EWSStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """EWS: Critical slowing down via rising variance + AC(1).</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; T0-01: Uses bank.get("ews_w") — independent window, not scalar_window.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._bank_registered = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._var_ewma = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ac1_ewma = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ews_score = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _ensure_bank(self, bank: WindowBank):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not self._bank_registered:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bank.register("ews_w", self.cfg.ews_window) &nbsp;# T0-01</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._bank_registered = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _ac1(self, data: List[float]) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(data)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if n &lt; 3:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu = _mean(data)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; num = sum((data[i] - mu) * (data[i+1] - mu) for i in range(n-1))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; den = sum((x - mu) ** 2 for x in data)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return (num / den) if den &gt; 1e-12 else 0.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ensure_bank(ctx.bank)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = list(ctx.bank.get("ews_w")) &nbsp;# T0-01: independent window</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(w) &lt; max(10, self.cfg.ews_window // 2):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ews_score"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ews_regime"] = "stable"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu = _mean(w)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; var = _mean([(x - mu) ** 2 for x in w])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ac1 = self._ac1(w)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alpha = 0.1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._var_ewma = alpha * var + (1 - alpha) * self._var_ewma</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ac1_ewma = alpha * ac1 + (1 - alpha) * self._ac1_ewma</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # EWS score: combine rising var + rising AC(1)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Both should be trending upward near a critical transition</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; var_trend = min(1.0, var / (self._var_ewma + 1e-10) if var &gt; 0 else 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ac1_clamped = max(0.0, min(1.0, self._ac1_ewma))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ews_score = 0.5 * var_trend + 0.5 * ac1_clamped</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thresh = self.cfg.ews_threshold</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._ews_score &gt; thresh * 1.5:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; regime = "critical"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif self._ews_score &gt; thresh:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; regime = "approaching"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; regime = "stable"</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ews_score"] = self._ews_score</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ews_regime"] = regime</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ews_var"] = var</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["ews_ac1"] = ac1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not ctx.is_warmup and regime == "critical":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"var_ewma": self._var_ewma, "ac1_ewma": self._ac1_ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "ews_score": self._ews_score, "n": self._n}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._var_ewma = sd.get("var_ewma", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ac1_ewma = sd.get("ac1_ewma", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._ews_score = sd.get("ews_score", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.15 AQBStep — Adaptive Quantile Baseline (FRM Axiom 1)</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class AQBStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """AQB: distribution-free quantile thresholds."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._buf: deque = deque(maxlen=self.cfg.aqb_window)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = ctx.current</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._buf.append(v)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(self._buf) &lt; 10 or not self.cfg.quantile_threshold_mode:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["aqb_lo"] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["aqb_hi"] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; s = sorted(self._buf)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(s)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lo_idx = max(0, int(self.cfg.aqb_q_low * n))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hi_idx = min(n - 1, int(self.cfg.aqb_q_high * n))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lo = s[lo_idx]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hi = s[hi_idx]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["aqb_lo"] = lo</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["aqb_hi"] = hi</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not ctx.is_warmup and (v &gt; hi or v &lt; lo):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"buf": list(self._buf)}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._buf = deque(sd.get("buf", []), maxlen=self.cfg.aqb_window)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.16 SeasonalStep — Seasonal Periodic Baseline</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class SeasonalStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Per-phase EWMA baseline; period auto-detected via FFT."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._period: Optional[int] = self.cfg.seasonal_period if self.cfg.seasonal_period &gt; 0 else None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._phase_ewma: Dict[int, float] = {}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._phase_dev: Dict[int, float] = {}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._detect_buf: List[float] = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _detect_period(self) -&gt; Optional[int]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not _NP or len(self._detect_buf) &lt; 32:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; arr = np.array(self._detect_buf)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; arr = arr - arr.mean()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; spec = np.abs(np.fft.rfft(arr)) ** 2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; freqs = np.fft.rfftfreq(len(arr))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(spec) &lt; 2:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; spec[0] = 0 &nbsp;# skip DC</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; peak_idx = int(np.argmax(spec))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if peak_idx == 0 or freqs[peak_idx] &lt; 1e-6:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; period = int(round(1.0 / freqs[peak_idx]))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return period if 2 &lt;= period &lt;= len(self._detect_buf) // 2 else None</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = ctx.current</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._period is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._detect_buf.append(v)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(self._detect_buf) &gt;= 64:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._period = self._detect_period()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["seasonal_err"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; phase = self._n % self._period</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alpha = self.cfg.alpha</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if phase not in self._phase_ewma:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._phase_ewma[phase] = v</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._phase_dev[phase] = 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prev = self._phase_ewma[phase]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._phase_ewma[phase] = alpha * v + (1 - alpha) * prev</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; err = abs(v - prev)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._phase_dev[phase] = 0.1 * err + 0.9 * self._phase_dev[phase]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; base = self._phase_ewma[phase]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dev = self._phase_dev[phase] or 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; err = abs(v - base) / dev</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["seasonal_err"] = err</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["seasonal_phase"] = phase</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["seasonal_period"] = self._period</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not ctx.is_warmup and err &gt; self.cfg.multiplier:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"period": self._period, "phase_ewma": self._phase_ewma,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "phase_dev": self._phase_dev, "n": self._n,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "detect_buf": self._detect_buf}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._period = sd.get("period")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._phase_ewma = {int(k): v for k, v in sd.get("phase_ewma", {}).items()}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._phase_dev = {int(k): v for k, v in sd.get("phase_dev", {}).items()}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._detect_buf = sd.get("detect_buf", [])</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.17 MahalStep — Mahalanobis distance (multivariate)</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class MahalStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Rolling EWMA covariance + Woodbury rank-1 update for Mahalanobis distance."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cov_inv = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._mean_vec = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not self.cfg.multivariate or not _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["mahal_dist"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = ctx.value</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not isinstance(v, (list, tuple)):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["mahal_dist"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; x = np.array([float(xi) for xi in v[:self.cfg.n_channels]])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; a = self.cfg.cov_alpha</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._mean_vec is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._mean_vec = x.copy()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; d = self.cfg.n_channels</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cov_inv = np.eye(d)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["mahal_dist"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # EWMA mean update</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._mean_vec = a * x + (1 - a) * self._mean_vec</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diff = x - self._mean_vec</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Woodbury rank-1 covariance inverse update</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # C_new = (1-a)*C + a * diff @ diff.T</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Use Sherman-Morrison: (A + uv^T)^{-1} = A^{-1} - (A^{-1}u v^T A^{-1})/(1 + v^T A^{-1} u)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; C_inv = self._cov_inv</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; u = diff.reshape(-1, 1)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; C_inv_u = C_inv @ u</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; denom = (1.0 - a) + a * float(u.T @ C_inv_u)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if abs(denom) &gt; 1e-12:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cov_inv = (C_inv - a * (C_inv_u @ C_inv_u.T) / denom) / (1.0 - a)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; d = self.cfg.n_channels</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cov_inv = np.eye(d)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Mahalanobis distance</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; md = float(math.sqrt(max(0.0, float(diff @ self._cov_inv @ diff))))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["mahal_dist"] = md</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thresh = self.cfg.multiplier * math.sqrt(self.cfg.n_channels)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not ctx.is_warmup and md &gt; thresh:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "mean_vec": self._mean_vec.tolist() if self._mean_vec is not None and _NP else None,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "cov_inv": self._cov_inv.tolist() if self._cov_inv is not None and _NP else None,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "n": self._n,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mv = sd.get("mean_vec")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ci = sd.get("cov_inv")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if mv is not None and _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._mean_vec = np.array(mv)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ci is not None and _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._cov_inv = np.array(ci)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.18 RRSStep — Rhythm Resonance Score (FRM Axiom 11)</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class RRSStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """RRS: harmonic resonance score — ratio of harmonic power to total power."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig, regime_step: Optional["RegimeStep"] = None):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._regime = regime_step</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = ctx.bank.get("scalar")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = self.cfg.rpi_window</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(w) &lt; n or not _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["rrs"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; arr = np.array(list(w)[-n:])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; arr = arr - arr.mean()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; spec = np.abs(np.fft.rfft(arr)) ** 2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; total = spec.sum()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if total &lt; 1e-12:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["rrs"] = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Fundamental: peak frequency; harmonics: 2x, 3x</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; peak_idx = int(np.argmax(spec[1:])) + 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; harm_power = spec[peak_idx]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for mult in [2, 3]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hi = peak_idx * mult</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if hi &lt; len(spec):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; harm_power += spec[hi]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rrs = float(harm_power / total)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["rrs"] = rrs</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"n": self._n}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># 5.19 AlertReasonsStep</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class AlertReasonsStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Aggregate alert reasons list — must be last step."""</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pass</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons: List[str] = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; s = ctx.scratch</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if s.get("cusum_alert"):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("cusum_mean_shift")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if s.get("var_cusum_alert"):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("cusum_variance_spike")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if s.get("regime_change"):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("regime_change")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if s.get("ph_alert"):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("gradual_drift")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if s.get("osc_alert"):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("oscillation_damping")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if s.get("cpd_score", 0) &gt; self.cfg.cpd_threshold:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("change_point")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if abs(s.get("z_score", 0)) &gt; self.cfg.multiplier:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("ewma_threshold")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if s.get("rfi", 0) &gt; self.cfg.rfi_threshold:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("high_fractal_irregularity")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ews = s.get("ews_regime", "stable")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ews in ("approaching", "critical"):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append(f"ews_{ews}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pe = s.get("pe", 0.5)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pe_base = s.get("pe_baseline", 0.5)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if abs(pe - pe_base) &gt; self.cfg.pe_threshold:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if pe &lt; pe_base:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("low_entropy_ordered")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("high_entropy_chaotic")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if s.get("mahal_dist", 0) &gt; self.cfg.multiplier * math.sqrt(self.cfg.n_channels):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append("mahalanobis_multivariate")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # V9.0 — include structured alert types in reasons list</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for alert in s.get("v9_active_alerts", []):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if alert.alert_type.value not in reasons:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reasons.append(alert.alert_type.value)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # V9.0 — compute channel summary string</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; channel_parts: List[str] = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if s.get("structural_snapshot") is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; channel_parts.append("structural:active")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if s.get("frequency_bands") is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; channel_parts.append("rhythmic:active")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cm = s.get("coupling_matrix")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if cm is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cst = ("degraded" if cm.composite_coupling_score &lt; self.cfg.coupling_degradation_threshold</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;else "healthy")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; channel_parts.append(f"coupling:{cst}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cc = s.get("channel_coherence")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if cc is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coh = "decoupled" if cc.coherence_score &lt; self.cfg.coherence_threshold else "coherent"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; channel_parts.append(f"coherence:{coh}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["channel_summary"] = (</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; " | ".join(channel_parts) if channel_parts else "channels:initializing"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert_reasons"] = reasons</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pass</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># V9.0 PIPELINE STEPS — Three-Channel Extension</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># V9 Step 4a: StructuralSnapshotStep — Channel 1</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class StructuralSnapshotStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Compute Channel 1 structural snapshot from current windowed data.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Step 4a — inserted immediately after CoreEWMAStep.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Treats network topology as active transmitter: computes statistical</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; properties of the input data stream as an independent information channel.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._snapshot_history: deque = deque(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; maxlen=max(self.cfg.coherence_window * 2, 40))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not (self.cfg.enable_channel_coherence or self.cfg.enable_cascade_detection):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["structural_snapshot"] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["_structural_snapshot_history"] = self._snapshot_history</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = list(ctx.bank.get("scalar"))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(w)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if n &lt; 4:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["structural_snapshot"] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["_structural_snapshot_history"] = self._snapshot_history</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mean = _mean(w)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; variance = _mean([(x - mean) ** 2 for x in w])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; std = math.sqrt(variance) if variance &gt; 1e-20 else 1e-10</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; skewness = (sum((x - mean) ** 3 for x in w) / (n * std ** 3)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if std &gt; 1e-10 else 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; kurtosis = (sum((x - mean) ** 4 for x in w) / (n * std ** 4) - 3</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if std &gt; 1e-10 else 0.0)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; denom = sum((x - mean) ** 2 for x in w)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ac1 = (sum((w[i] - mean) * (w[i - 1] - mean) for i in range(1, n)) / denom</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;if denom &gt; 1e-20 else 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ac2 = (sum((w[i] - mean) * (w[i - 2] - mean) for i in range(2, n)) / denom</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;if denom &gt; 1e-20 else 0.0)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; half = n // 2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if half &gt; 1:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu1 = _mean(w[:half])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu2 = _mean(w[half:])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v1 = _mean([(x - mu1) ** 2 for x in w[:half]])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v2 = _mean([(x - mu2) ** 2 for x in w[half:]])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stationarity = 1.0 - abs(v2 - v1) / (v1 + v2 + 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stationarity = 1.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; snapshot = StructuralSnapshot(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mean=mean,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; variance=variance,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; skewness=skewness,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; kurtosis=kurtosis,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; autocorrelation_lag1=ac1,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; autocorrelation_lag2=ac2,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stationarity_score=max(0.0, min(1.0, stationarity)),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; timestamp=ctx.step,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._snapshot_history.append(snapshot)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["structural_snapshot"] = snapshot</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["_structural_snapshot_history"] = self._snapshot_history</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"n_snapshots": len(self._snapshot_history)}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pass &nbsp;# in-memory history only</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># V9 Step 4b: FrequencyDecompositionStep — Channel 2</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class FrequencyDecompositionStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Decompose windowed signal into five frequency band carrier waves.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Step 4b — inserted immediately after StructuralSnapshotStep.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Implements Channel 2: broadband multiplexed oscillatory transmission.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Uses numpy FFT if available; falls back to pure-Python DFT.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._bands_history: deque = deque(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; maxlen=max(self.cfg.coupling_trend_window * 4, 60))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _pure_python_bands(self, data: List[float]) -&gt; tuple:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; N = len(data)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; spectrum = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for k in range(N // 2 + 1):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; re = sum(data[t] * math.cos(2 * math.pi * k * t / N) for t in range(N))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; im = sum(data[t] * math.sin(2 * math.pi * k * t / N) for t in range(N))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mag = math.sqrt(re ** 2 + im ** 2)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; phase = math.atan2(-im, re)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; spectrum.append((mag, phase))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; total = len(spectrum)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; def pure_band(lo_frac, hi_frac):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lo_i = int(lo_frac * total)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hi_i = int(hi_frac * total)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if hi_i &lt;= lo_i:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.0, 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; s = spectrum[lo_i:hi_i]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; avg_mag = sum(x[0] for x in s) / len(s)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; avg_phase = sum(x[1] for x in s) / len(s)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return avg_mag, avg_phase</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ul_p, ul_ph = pure_band(0.00, 0.05)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; l_p, &nbsp;l_ph &nbsp;= pure_band(0.05, 0.15)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; m_p, &nbsp;m_ph &nbsp;= pure_band(0.15, 0.40)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; h_p, &nbsp;h_ph &nbsp;= pure_band(0.40, 0.70)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; uh_p, uh_ph = pure_band(0.70, 1.00)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return ul_p, ul_ph, l_p, l_ph, m_p, m_ph, h_p, h_ph, uh_p, uh_ph</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _compute_bands(self, data: List[float], timestamp: int) -&gt; Optional[FrequencyBands]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(data)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; import numpy as _np_local</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; arr = _np_local.array(data, dtype=float)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fft = _np_local.fft.rfft(arr)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; freqs = _np_local.fft.rfftfreq(n)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; magnitudes = _np_local.abs(fft)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; phases = _np_local.angle(fft)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; def band_stats(lo, hi):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mask = (freqs &gt;= lo) &amp; (freqs &lt; hi)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not _np_local.any(mask):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.0, 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return float(_np_local.mean(magnitudes[mask])), float(_np_local.mean(phases[mask]))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ul_p, ul_ph = band_stats(0.00, 0.05)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; l_p, &nbsp;l_ph &nbsp;= band_stats(0.05, 0.15)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; m_p, &nbsp;m_ph &nbsp;= band_stats(0.15, 0.40)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; h_p, &nbsp;h_ph &nbsp;= band_stats(0.40, 0.70)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; uh_p, uh_ph = band_stats(0.70, 1.00)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; except ImportError:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ul_p, ul_ph, l_p, l_ph, m_p, m_ph, h_p, h_ph, uh_p, uh_ph = \</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pure_python_bands(data)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return FrequencyBands(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ultra_low_power=ul_p, low_power=l_p, mid_power=m_p,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; high_power=h_p, ultra_high_power=uh_p,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ultra_low_phase=ul_ph, low_phase=l_ph, mid_phase=m_ph,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; high_phase=h_ph, ultra_high_phase=uh_ph,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; timestamp=timestamp,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not self.cfg.enable_frequency_decomposition:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["frequency_bands"] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["_bands_history"] = self._bands_history</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; w = list(ctx.bank.get("scalar"))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(w)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if n &lt; self.cfg.min_window_for_fft:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["frequency_bands"] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["_bands_history"] = self._bands_history</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bands = self._compute_bands(w, ctx.step)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if bands is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._bands_history.append(bands)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["frequency_bands"] = bands</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["_bands_history"] = self._bands_history</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"n_bands": len(self._bands_history)}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pass &nbsp;# in-memory history only</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># V9 Step 15a: BandAnomalyStep</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class BandAnomalyStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Per-carrier-wave anomaly detection invisible to composite signal.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Step 15a — run after existing detection steps.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Applies independent EWMA anomaly detection to each frequency band's</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; power time series. A band-specific anomaly not present in the composite</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; signal is invisible to v8.0 but detectable here.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; BAND_NAMES: List[str] = ["ultra_low", "low", "mid", "high", "ultra_high"]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._band_ewma: Dict[str, float] = {}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._band_dev: Dict[str, float] = {}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _ewma_anomaly_score(self, power: float, band_name: str) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Return normalized anomaly score (&gt;1.0 = anomalous) for a band."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alpha = self.cfg.alpha</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if band_name not in self._band_ewma:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._band_ewma[band_name] = power</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._band_dev[band_name] = 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prev = self._band_ewma[band_name]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._band_ewma[band_name] = alpha * power + (1 - alpha) * prev</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; err = abs(power - prev)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._band_dev[band_name] = (</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alpha * err + (1 - alpha) * self._band_dev.get(band_name, 1.0))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._band_dev[band_name] = max(self._band_dev[band_name], 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; z = abs(power - self._band_ewma[band_name]) / self._band_dev[band_name]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return z / (self.cfg.multiplier + 1e-10)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fb = ctx.scratch.get("frequency_bands")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if fb is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["band_anomalies"] = {}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch.setdefault("v9_active_alerts", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; current_powers = [</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fb.ultra_low_power, fb.low_power, fb.mid_power,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fb.high_power, fb.ultra_high_power,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; anomalies: Dict[str, float] = {}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for name, power in zip(self.BAND_NAMES, current_powers):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; score = self._ewma_anomaly_score(power, name)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if score &gt; 1.0:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; anomalies[name] = min(1.0, score)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["band_anomalies"] = anomalies</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alerts: List[Alert] = list(ctx.scratch.get("v9_active_alerts", []))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if anomalies and not ctx.is_warmup and not ctx.scratch.get("alert", False):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Per-band anomaly not present in composite — new information</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert = Alert(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert_type=AlertType.BAND_ANOMALY,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; severity=AlertSeverity.WARNING,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; score=max(anomalies.values()),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; message=(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Per-band anomaly in bands: {sorted(anomalies.keys())}. "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Invisible to composite detection."</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alerts.append(alert)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["v9_active_alerts"] = alerts</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"band_ewma": dict(self._band_ewma), "band_dev": dict(self._band_dev)}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._band_ewma = sd.get("band_ewma", {})</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._band_dev = sd.get("band_dev", {})</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># V9 Steps 15b+15c: CrossFrequencyCouplingStep</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class CrossFrequencyCouplingStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Measure cross-frequency phase-amplitude coupling and detect degradation.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Step 15b+15c — computes CouplingMatrix and generates COUPLING_DEGRADATION</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; alert when composite_coupling_score falls below threshold.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Earlier warning than single-band anomaly detection.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._coupling_degradation_active: bool = False</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @staticmethod</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _pac(low_phases: List[float], high_powers: List[float]) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Phase-amplitude coupling: modulation index approximation."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(low_phases)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if n &lt; 2:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bins: List[List[float]] = [[] for _ in range(8)]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for ph, pw in zip(low_phases, high_powers):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bin_idx = int((ph + math.pi) / (2 * math.pi) * 8) % 8</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bins[bin_idx].append(pw)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bin_means = [sum(b) / len(b) if b else 0.0 for b in bins]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; overall_mean = sum(bin_means) / 8.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; variance = sum((m - overall_mean) ** 2 for m in bin_means) / 8.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; best_dev = max(bin_means) - overall_mean</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; max_variance = best_dev ** 2 if best_dev &gt; 0 else 1e-10</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return variance / (max_variance + 1e-10)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _composite_from_slice(self, bands_slice: list) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(bands_slice) &lt; 2:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return sum([</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pac([b.ultra_low_phase for b in bands_slice],</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; [b.low_power for b in bands_slice]),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pac([b.low_phase for b in bands_slice],</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; [b.mid_power for b in bands_slice]),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pac([b.mid_phase for b in bands_slice],</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; [b.high_power for b in bands_slice]),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pac([b.high_phase for b in bands_slice],</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; [b.ultra_high_power for b in bands_slice]),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ]) / 4.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not self.cfg.enable_coupling_detection:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["coupling_matrix"] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["coupling_degradation_active"] = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._coupling_degradation_active = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch.setdefault("v9_active_alerts", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bands_history = ctx.scratch.get("_bands_history")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if bands_history is None or len(bands_history) &lt; self.cfg.coupling_trend_window:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["coupling_matrix"] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["coupling_degradation_active"] = self._coupling_degradation_active</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch.setdefault("v9_active_alerts", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; recent = list(bands_history)[-self.cfg.coupling_trend_window:]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ul_phases = [b.ultra_low_phase for b in recent]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; l_phases &nbsp;= [b.low_phase for b in recent]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; m_phases &nbsp;= [b.mid_phase for b in recent]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; h_phases &nbsp;= [b.high_phase for b in recent]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; l_powers &nbsp;= [b.low_power for b in recent]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; m_powers &nbsp;= [b.mid_power for b in recent]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; h_powers &nbsp;= [b.high_power for b in recent]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; uh_powers = [b.ultra_high_power for b in recent]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ul_to_l = self._pac(ul_phases, l_powers)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; l_to_m &nbsp;= self._pac(l_phases, &nbsp;m_powers)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; m_to_h &nbsp;= self._pac(m_phases, &nbsp;h_powers)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; h_to_uh = self._pac(h_phases, &nbsp;uh_powers)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; composite = (ul_to_l + l_to_m + m_to_h + h_to_uh) / 4.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; half = len(recent) // 2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if half &gt;= 2:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; early = self._composite_from_slice(recent[:half])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; late &nbsp;= self._composite_from_slice(recent[half:])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; trend = late - early</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; trend = 0.0</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coupling = CouplingMatrix(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ultra_low_to_low=ul_to_l,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; low_to_mid=l_to_m,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mid_to_high=m_to_h,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; high_to_ultra_high=h_to_uh,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; composite_coupling_score=composite,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coupling_trend=trend,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; timestamp=ctx.step,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["coupling_matrix"] = coupling</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alerts: List[Alert] = list(ctx.scratch.get("v9_active_alerts", []))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if composite &lt; self.cfg.coupling_degradation_threshold and not ctx.is_warmup:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._coupling_degradation_active = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert = Alert(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert_type=AlertType.COUPLING_DEGRADATION,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; severity=AlertSeverity.WARNING,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; score=composite,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; message=(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Cross-frequency coupling degraded to {composite:.3f} "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"(threshold: {self.cfg.coupling_degradation_threshold}). "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Trend: {trend:+.3f}. Heterodyned information channel at risk."</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alerts.append(alert)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._coupling_degradation_active = False</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["coupling_degradation_active"] = self._coupling_degradation_active</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["v9_active_alerts"] = alerts</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def state_dict(self) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"coupling_degradation_active": self._coupling_degradation_active}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, sd: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._coupling_degradation_active = sd.get("coupling_degradation_active", False)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div># V9 Steps 15d+15e: ChannelCoherenceStep</div><div># ---------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>@register_step</div><div>class ChannelCoherenceStep(DetectorStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Measure structural-rhythmic channel coherence and detect decoupling.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Step 15d+15e — computes ChannelCoherence and generates</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; STRUCTURAL_RHYTHMIC_DECOUPLING alert when coherence_score falls below</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; coherence_threshold. Independent of anomalies in either individual channel.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: SentinelConfig):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.cfg = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._rhythmic_history: deque = deque(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; maxlen=self.cfg.coherence_window * 2)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._sr_decoupling_active: bool = False</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _coherence_score_from_slices(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self, struct_slice: list, rhythmic_slice: list</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(struct_slice) &lt; 2 or len(rhythmic_slice) &lt; 2:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.5</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = min(len(struct_slice), len(rhythmic_slice))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ss = struct_slice[-n:]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rs = rhythmic_slice[-n:]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sc = [abs(ss[i].variance - ss[i - 1].variance) for i in range(1, len(ss))]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rc = [abs(rs[i] - rs[i - 1]) for i in range(1, len(rs))]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; s_rate = _mean(sc) if sc else 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; r_rate = _mean(rc) if rc else 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; max_rate = max(s_rate, r_rate, 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return max(0.0, min(1.0, 1.0 - abs(s_rate - r_rate) / max_rate))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, ctx: StepContext) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not self.cfg.enable_channel_coherence:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["channel_coherence"] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["sr_decoupling_active"] = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._sr_decoupling_active = False</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch.setdefault("v9_active_alerts", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Accumulate rhythmic proxy (EWMA value)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._rhythmic_history.append(ctx.scratch.get("ewma", ctx.current))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; structural_history = ctx.scratch.get("_structural_snapshot_history")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; window = self.cfg.coherence_window</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (structural_history is None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; or len(structural_history) &lt; window</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; or len(self._rhythmic_history) &lt; window):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["channel_coherence"] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["sr_decoupling_active"] = self._sr_decoupling_active</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch.setdefault("v9_active_alerts", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; recent_struct = list(structural_history)[-window:]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; recent_rhythmic = list(self._rhythmic_history)[-window:]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sc = [abs(recent_struct[i].variance - recent_struct[i - 1].variance)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in range(1, len(recent_struct))]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rc = [abs(recent_rhythmic[i] - recent_rhythmic[i - 1])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in range(1, len(recent_rhythmic))]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; structural_change_rate = _mean(sc) if sc else 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rhythmic_change_rate = _mean(rc) if rc else 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; max_rate = max(structural_change_rate, rhythmic_change_rate, 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coherence_score = max(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 0.0, min(1.0, 1.0 - abs(structural_change_rate - rhythmic_change_rate) / max_rate)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; half = window // 2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; early_coh = self._coherence_score_from_slices(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; recent_struct[:half], recent_rhythmic[:half])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; late_coh = self._coherence_score_from_slices(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; recent_struct[half:], recent_rhythmic[half:])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; decoupling_trend = late_coh - early_coh</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coherence = ChannelCoherence(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coherence_score=coherence_score,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; structural_change_rate=structural_change_rate,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rhythmic_change_rate=rhythmic_change_rate,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; decoupling_trend=decoupling_trend,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; timestamp=ctx.step,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["channel_coherence"] = coherence</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alerts: List[Alert] = list(ctx.scratch.get("v9_active_alerts", []))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if coherence_score &lt; self.cfg.coherence_threshold and not ctx.is_warmup:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._sr_decoupling_active = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert = Alert(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alert_type=AlertType.STRUCTURAL_RHYTHMIC_DECOUPLING,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; severity=AlertSeverity.ALERT,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; score=coherence_score,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; message=(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Channel 1-2 coherence degraded to {coherence_score:.3f} "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"(threshold: {self.cfg.coherence_threshold}). "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Structural rate: {structural_change_rate:.4f}. "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Rhythmic rate: {rhythmic_change_rate:.4f}. "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Channels operating independently."</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alerts.append(alert)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["alert"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["anomaly"] = True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._sr_decoupling_active = False</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; """Returns status of each channel: healthy, degrading, anomalous, or unknown."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status: Dict[str, str] = {}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
