&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["structural"] = "anomalous"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif ss.stationarity_score &lt; 0.6:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["structural"] = "degrading"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["structural"] = "healthy"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["structural"] = "unknown"</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; score = self.get("anomaly_score", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if score &gt;= 1.0:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["rhythmic_composite"] = "anomalous"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif score &gt; 0.5:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["rhythmic_composite"] = "degrading"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["rhythmic_composite"] = "healthy"</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cm = self.get("coupling_matrix")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if cm is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if cm.coupling_trend &lt; -0.1:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["coupling"] = "degrading"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif cm.composite_coupling_score &lt; 0.3:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["coupling"] = "anomalous"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["coupling"] = "healthy"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["coupling"] = "unknown"</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cc = self.get("channel_coherence")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if cc is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if cc.coherence_score &lt; 0.2:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["coherence"] = "anomalous"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif cc.coherence_score &lt; 0.4:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["coherence"] = "degrading"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["coherence"] = "healthy"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status["coherence"] = "unknown"</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return status</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def get_degradation_narrative(self) -&gt; str:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Returns human-readable description of current degradation sequence."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ds = self.get("degradation_sequence")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ds is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return ds.sequence_pattern</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return "No active degradation sequence."</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def get_primary_carrier_wave(self) -&gt; str:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Returns frequency band currently carrying the most information."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fb = self.get("frequency_bands")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if fb is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return "decomposition_disabled"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bands = {</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "ultra_low": fb.ultra_low_power,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "low": fb.low_power,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "mid": fb.mid_power,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "high": fb.high_power,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "ultra_high": fb.ultra_high_power,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return max(bands, key=bands.get)</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># SECTION 6 — SentinelDetector (main orchestrator)</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div>class SentinelDetector:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Streaming anomaly detector — v8.0 pipeline architecture.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Usage::</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; det = SentinelDetector()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for value in stream:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result = det.update_and_check(value)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if result["alert"]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(result["alert_reasons"])</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Backward-compatible with all v7.x kwargs.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ``Detector_7_10`` is an alias for this class.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: Optional[SentinelConfig] = None,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;*, steps: Optional[List[DetectorStep]] = None,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;**legacy_kwargs):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if config is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if legacy_kwargs:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; config = _legacy_kwargs_to_config(legacy_kwargs)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; config = SentinelConfig()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.config = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._bank = WindowBank()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if steps is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pipeline = list(steps)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pipeline = _build_default_pipeline(config)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Wire CoreEWMAStep reference into scratch for RegimeStep soft-boost</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._core_step: Optional[CoreEWMAStep] = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for s in self._pipeline:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if isinstance(s, CoreEWMAStep):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._core_step = s</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; break</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._history: deque = deque(maxlen=config.history_maxlen)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_file = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_writer = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if config.csv_path:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._open_csv(config.csv_path)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # Core API</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update_and_check(self, value) -&gt; "SentinelResult":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Process one observation; return SentinelResult (dict subclass)."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx = StepContext(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; value=value,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; step=self._n,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; config=self.config,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bank=self._bank,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; scratch={},</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Inject core step ref for regime soft-boost</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._core_step is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ctx.scratch["_core_step_ref"] = self._core_step</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for step in self._pipeline:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; step.update(ctx)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result = SentinelResult(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; (k, v) for k, v in ctx.scratch.items()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not k.startswith("_")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("alert", False)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("anomaly", False)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("warmup", ctx.is_warmup)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("z_score", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("anomaly_score", 0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("alert_reasons", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # V9.0 defaults</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("frequency_bands", None)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("structural_snapshot", None)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("coupling_matrix", None)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("channel_coherence", None)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("degradation_sequence", None)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("cascade_precursor_active", False)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("band_anomalies", {})</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("channel_summary", "")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result.setdefault("v9_active_alerts", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result["step"] = self._n</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result["value"] = value if not isinstance(value, (list, tuple)) else list(value)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._history.append(result)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._csv_writer is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._write_csv_row(result)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return result</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; async def aupdate(self, value) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Async wrapper for update_and_check."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self.update_and_check(value)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # Fitting / tuning</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def fit(self, data: Sequence) -&gt; "SentinelDetector":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Warm up detector on unlabeled data (returns self)."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for v in data:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.update_and_check(v)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; @classmethod</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def auto_tune(cls, data: Sequence,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; labeled_data: Optional[Sequence[Tuple[Any, bool]]] = None,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alphas: Optional[List[float]] = None,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; multipliers: Optional[List[float]] = None) -&gt; "SentinelDetector":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Grid-search alpha/multiplier to maximise F1 on labeled_data</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; (or minimise false-positive rate if labels not provided).</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if alphas is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alphas = [0.05, 0.1, 0.2, 0.3]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if multipliers is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; multipliers = [2.0, 2.5, 3.0, 3.5, 4.0]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; best_score = -1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; best_cfg: Optional[SentinelConfig] = None</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for a in alphas:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for m in multipliers:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cfg = SentinelConfig(alpha=a, dev_alpha=a, multiplier=m)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; det = cls(config=cfg)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if labeled_data is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; results = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; labels = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for v, lbl in labeled_data:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; r = det.update_and_check(v)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; results.append(r)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; labels.append(lbl)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Compute F1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tp = fp = fn = 0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for r, lbl in zip(results, labels):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pred = r["alert"]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if pred and lbl: tp += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif pred and not lbl: fp += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif not pred and lbl: fn += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prec = tp / (tp + fp + 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rec = tp / (tp + fn + 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f1 = 2 * prec * rec / (prec + rec + 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; score = f1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; results = [det.update_and_check(v) for v in data]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fp_rate = sum(1 for r in results if r["alert"] and not r["warmup"]) / (len(results) + 1)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; score = 1.0 - fp_rate</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if score &gt; best_score:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; best_score = score</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; best_cfg = cfg</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return cls(config=best_cfg or SentinelConfig())</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # State persistence</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def save_state(self) -&gt; str:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Serialize full detector state to JSON string."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sd: Dict[str, Any] = {</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "version": __version__,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "n": self._n,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "config": dataclasses.asdict(self.config),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "bank": self._bank.state_dict(),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "steps": [],</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i, step in enumerate(self._pipeline):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sd["steps"].append({</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "cls": type(step).__name__,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "idx": i,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "state": step.state_dict(),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; })</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return json.dumps(sd)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_state(self, json_str: str) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Restore detector state from JSON string."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sd = json.loads(json_str)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = sd.get("n", 0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._bank.load_state(sd.get("bank", {}))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; step_states = sd.get("steps", [])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for ss in step_states:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; idx = ss.get("idx", -1)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if 0 &lt;= idx &lt; len(self._pipeline):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._pipeline[idx].load_state(ss.get("state", {}))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # Reset</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset(self, soft: bool = False) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Reset detector state.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Parameters</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ----------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soft:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; If True, only reset accumulators but keep warmup data.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; If False (default), full reset to factory state.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._n = 0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._history.clear()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._bank.reset()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for step in self._pipeline:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; step.reset()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # CSV / history</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _open_csv(self, path: str) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_file = open(path, "w", newline="")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_writer = None &nbsp;# created lazily on first row</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _write_csv_row(self, result: Dict[str, Any]) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._csv_writer is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fieldnames = [k for k in result.keys() if k != "alert_reasons"]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fieldnames.append("alert_reasons")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_writer = csv.DictWriter(self._csv_file, fieldnames=fieldnames,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;extrasaction="ignore")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_writer.writeheader()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; row = dict(result)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; row["alert_reasons"] = "|".join(result.get("alert_reasons", []))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_writer.writerow(row)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_file.flush()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def flush_csv(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Flush pending CSV writes."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._csv_file is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_file.flush()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def close(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Close CSV file if open."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._csv_file is not None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_file.close()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_file = None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._csv_writer = None</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # Plotting</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def plot_history(self, title: str = "Sentinel v8 Dashboard",</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;show: bool = True) -&gt; Optional[Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """4-panel dashboard: value+EWMA, anomaly_score, PE, z_score."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not _MPL:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; warnings.warn("matplotlib not available")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return None</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; history = list(self._history)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not history:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return None</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; steps = [r["step"] for r in history]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; values = [r.get("value", 0) if not isinstance(r.get("value"), list) else r["value"][-1]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for r in history]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ewmas = [r.get("ewma", 0) for r in history]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; scores = [r.get("anomaly_score", 0) for r in history]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pes = [r.get("pe", 0.5) for r in history]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; zs = [r.get("z_score", 0) for r in history]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alerts = [i for i, r in enumerate(history) if r.get("alert")]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fig, axes = plt.subplots(4, 1, figsize=(14, 10), sharex=True)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fig.suptitle(title, fontsize=14, fontweight="bold")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[0].plot(steps, values, color="steelblue", linewidth=0.8, label="Value")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[0].plot(steps, ewmas, color="orange", linewidth=1.5, label="EWMA")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for ai in alerts:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[0].axvline(steps[ai], color="red", alpha=0.3, linewidth=0.5)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[0].set_ylabel("Value / EWMA")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[0].legend(fontsize=8)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[1].plot(steps, scores, color="purple", linewidth=0.8)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[1].axhline(1.0, color="red", linestyle="--", linewidth=0.8)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[1].set_ylabel("Anomaly Score")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[2].plot(steps, pes, color="teal", linewidth=0.8)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[2].set_ylabel("Permutation Entropy")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[3].plot(steps, zs, color="gray", linewidth=0.8)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[3].axhline(self.config.multiplier, color="red", linestyle="--", linewidth=0.8)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[3].axhline(-self.config.multiplier, color="red", linestyle="--", linewidth=0.8)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[3].set_ylabel("Z-score")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; axes[3].set_xlabel("Step")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; plt.tight_layout()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if show:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; plt.show()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return fig</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # Dunder helpers</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __repr__(self) -&gt; str:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return (f"SentinelDetector(v{__version__}, n={self._n}, "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"alpha={self.config.alpha}, warmup={self.config.warmup_periods}, "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"three_channel=True)")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __len__(self) -&gt; int:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self._n</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># Backward-compat alias (ε)</div><div>Detector_7_10 = SentinelDetector</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># SECTION 7 — MultiStreamSentinel</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div>class MultiStreamSentinel:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Manage multiple independent named streams, each with its own detector.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Each stream is lazily initialized on first observation. &nbsp;Streams share</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; a common ``config`` but have fully independent state.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, config: Optional[SentinelConfig] = None,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;detector_factory: Optional[Callable] = None,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;**legacy_kwargs):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if config is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if legacy_kwargs:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; config = _legacy_kwargs_to_config(legacy_kwargs)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; config = SentinelConfig()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.config = config</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._factory = detector_factory or (lambda cfg: SentinelDetector(config=cfg))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._streams: Dict[str, SentinelDetector] = {}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._lock = threading.Lock()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def update(self, stream_id: str, value) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Update a named stream; auto-create detector on first call."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; with self._lock:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if stream_id not in self._streams:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._streams[stream_id] = self._factory(self.config)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self._streams[stream_id].update_and_check(value)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; async def aupdate(self, stream_id: str, value) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Async variant of update."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self.update(stream_id, value)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def get_detector(self, stream_id: str) -&gt; Optional[SentinelDetector]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self._streams.get(stream_id)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def list_streams(self) -&gt; List[str]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return list(self._streams.keys())</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def reset_stream(self, stream_id: str) -&gt; bool:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Reset a named stream; return False if not found."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if stream_id in self._streams:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._streams[stream_id].reset()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return False</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def delete_stream(self, stream_id: str) -&gt; bool:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Delete a named stream; return False if not found."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; with self._lock:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if stream_id in self._streams:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._streams.pop(stream_id)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return True</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return False</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def status(self, stream_id: str) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; det = self._streams.get(stream_id)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if det is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"error": "stream not found"}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; history = list(det._history)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alerts = sum(1 for r in history if r.get("alert"))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "stream_id": stream_id,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "n": det._n,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "alert_count": alerts,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "last_result": history[-1] if history else None,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def save_all(self) -&gt; str:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Serialize all stream states to JSON string."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return json.dumps({</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sid: json.loads(det.save_state())</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for sid, det in self._streams.items()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; })</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def load_all(self, json_str: str) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Restore all stream states from JSON string."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; data = json.loads(json_str)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for sid, sd in data.items():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if sid not in self._streams:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._streams[sid] = self._factory(self.config)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._streams[sid].load_state(json.dumps(sd))</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __repr__(self) -&gt; str:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return f"MultiStreamSentinel(streams={list(self._streams.keys())})"</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># SECTION 8 — SentinelBenchmark</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div>class SentinelBenchmark:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Built-in evaluation harness.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Generates five labeled anomaly archetypes and reports F1, AUPRC (PR curve</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; via trapezoidal integration), VUS-PR (avg AUPRC over 5 buffer tolerances),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; mean detection lag, and naive 3-sigma baseline comparison.</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ARCHETYPES: List[str] = ["point", "contextual", "collective", "drift", "variance"]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, n: int = 500, seed: int = 42,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;config: Optional[SentinelConfig] = None):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.n = n</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.seed = seed</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.config = config or SentinelConfig()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._rng: Any = None</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _get_rng(self) -&gt; Any:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if self._rng is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._rng = np.random.default_rng(self.seed)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; import random</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; random.seed(self.seed)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._rng = random</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return self._rng</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _randn(self, n: int) -&gt; List[float]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rng = self._get_rng()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if _NP:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return rng.standard_normal(n).tolist()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; import random</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return [random.gauss(0, 1) for _ in range(n)]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def generate(self, archetype: str) -&gt; Tuple[List[float], List[bool]]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Generate (data, labels) for a given archetype."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = self.n</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; data = self._randn(n)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; labels = [False] * n</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if archetype == "point":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Sparse large spikes</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; idxs = list(range(50, n, 80))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in idxs:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if i &lt; n:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; data[i] += 8.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; labels[i] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif archetype == "contextual":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Normal values that are anomalous given seasonal context</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; period = 20</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in range(n):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Add sinusoidal mean</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; data[i] += 3.0 * math.sin(2 * math.pi * i / period)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; idxs = list(range(60, n, 100))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in idxs:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if i &lt; n:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; data[i] = data[i] - 6.0 &nbsp;# contextually anomalous</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; labels[i] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif archetype == "collective":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Runs of anomalous observations</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; idxs = list(range(100, 120)) + list(range(300, 315))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in idxs:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if i &lt; n:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; data[i] += 4.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; labels[i] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif archetype == "drift":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Slow mean drift</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in range(n):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if i &gt; n // 2:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; data[i] += (i - n // 2) * 0.02</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in range(n // 2 + 20, n):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; labels[i] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif archetype == "variance":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Sudden variance explosion</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in range(n // 2, n):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; data[i] *= 4.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; labels[i] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; raise ValueError(f"Unknown archetype: {archetype}")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return data, labels</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _pr_auc(self, scores: List[float], labels: List[bool],</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tolerance: int = 0) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Trapezoidal AUPRC with buffer tolerance."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; n = len(scores)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Expand labels with tolerance</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tol_labels = list(labels)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if tolerance &gt; 0:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i, lbl in enumerate(labels):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if lbl:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for j in range(max(0, i - tolerance), min(n, i + tolerance + 1)):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tol_labels[j] = True</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paired = sorted(zip(scores, tol_labels), key=lambda x: -x[0])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tp = fp = 0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; total_pos = sum(1 for lbl in tol_labels if lbl)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if total_pos == 0:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; precs = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; recs = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for score, lbl in paired:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if lbl:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tp += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fp += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; precs.append(tp / (tp + fp))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; recs.append(tp / total_pos)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Trapezoidal integration</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; auc = 0.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i in range(1, len(precs)):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; auc += (recs[i] - recs[i-1]) * (precs[i] + precs[i-1]) / 2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return max(0.0, auc)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _vus_pr(self, scores: List[float], labels: List[bool]) -&gt; float:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Volume Under PR Surface over tolerances {0,5,10,15,20}."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tols = [0, 5, 10, 15, 20]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return sum(self._pr_auc(scores, labels, t) for t in tols) / len(tols)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def _naive_baseline(self, data: List[float], labels: List[bool]) -&gt; Dict[str, float]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """3-sigma naive baseline."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mu = _mean(data)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sq = [(x - mu) ** 2 for x in data]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; std = math.sqrt(_mean(sq)) or 1.0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; preds = [abs(x - mu) &gt; 3 * std for x in data]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tp = sum(1 for p, l in zip(preds, labels) if p and l)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fp = sum(1 for p, l in zip(preds, labels) if p and not l)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fn = sum(1 for p, l in zip(preds, labels) if not p and l)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prec = tp / (tp + fp + 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rec = tp / (tp + fn + 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f1 = 2 * prec * rec / (prec + rec + 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {"f1": f1, "precision": prec, "recall": rec}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def evaluate(self, archetype: str) -&gt; Dict[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Run detector on one archetype; return metrics dict."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; data, labels = self.generate(archetype)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; det = SentinelDetector(config=self.config)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; results = [det.update_and_check(v) for v in data]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; scores = [r.get("anomaly_score", 0.0) for r in results]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; preds = [r.get("alert", False) for r in results]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # F1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tp = fp = fn = 0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; detection_lags = []</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for i, (pred, lbl) in enumerate(zip(preds, labels)):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if pred and lbl: tp += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif pred and not lbl: fp += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elif not pred and lbl: fn += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prec = tp / (tp + fp + 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rec = tp / (tp + fn + 1e-10)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f1 = 2 * prec * rec / (prec + rec + 1e-10)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Detection lag for true anomalies</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; anom_starts = [i for i, l in enumerate(labels) if l and (i == 0 or not labels[i-1])]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for start in anom_starts:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for j in range(start, min(start + 50, len(preds))):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if preds[j]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; detection_lags.append(j - start)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; break</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; auprc = self._pr_auc(scores, labels)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vus = self._vus_pr(scores, labels)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; naive = self._naive_baseline(data, labels)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mean_lag = _mean(detection_lags) if detection_lags else float("inf")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return {</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "archetype": archetype,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "f1": f1,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "precision": prec,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "recall": rec,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "auprc": auprc,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "vus_pr": vus,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "mean_lag": mean_lag,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "naive_f1": naive["f1"],</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "n_alerts": sum(preds),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "n_true_anomalies": sum(labels),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def run_suite(self, verbose: bool = True) -&gt; Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Run all 5 archetypes; print summary table."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; results = {}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for arch in self.ARCHETYPES:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; results[arch] = self.evaluate(arch)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if verbose:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(f"\n{'─'*72}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(f"{'Sentinel v8 Benchmark':^72}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(f"{'─'*72}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; header = f"{'Archetype':&lt;14} {'F1':&gt;6} {'AUPRC':&gt;7} {'VUS-PR':&gt;7} "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; header += f"{'Lag':&gt;6} {'Naive F1':&gt;9} {'Alerts':&gt;7}"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(header)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(f"{'─'*72}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for arch, r in results.items():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lag = f"{r['mean_lag']:.1f}" if r['mean_lag'] != float('inf') else "∞"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(f"{arch:&lt;14} {r['f1']:&gt;6.3f} {r['auprc']:&gt;7.3f} {r['vus_pr']:&gt;7.3f} "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"{lag:&gt;6} {r['naive_f1']:&gt;9.3f} {r['n_alerts']:&gt;7}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(f"{'─'*72}\n")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return results</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># SECTION 9 — SentinelServer (asyncio)</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div>class SentinelServer:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """Async HTTP server wrapping MultiStreamSentinel.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; Endpoints:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; POST /update/&lt;stream_id&gt; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; body: {"value": ...}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; GET &nbsp;/streams &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;returns list of stream IDs</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; GET &nbsp;/status/&lt;stream_id&gt; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; returns stream status</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; DELETE /stream/&lt;stream_id&gt; &nbsp; &nbsp; delete a stream</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; POST /reset/&lt;stream_id&gt; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;reset a stream</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; GET &nbsp;/health &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; version + uptime</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; """</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def __init__(self, host: str = "0.0.0.0", port: int = 8765,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;config: Optional[SentinelConfig] = None):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.host = host</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.port = port</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self.mss = MultiStreamSentinel(config=config)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._start_time = time.time()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._server: Optional[Any] = None</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; async def _handle(self, reader: asyncio.StreamReader,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writer: asyncio.StreamWriter) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; raw = await asyncio.wait_for(reader.read(65536), timeout=5.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lines = raw.decode("utf-8", errors="replace").split("\r\n")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not lines:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writer.close()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; req_line = lines[0].split()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if len(req_line) &lt; 2:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writer.close()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; method = req_line[0].upper()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; path = req_line[1]</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; # Find body (after blank line)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; body_str = ""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sep = raw.index(b"\r\n\r\n")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; body_str = raw[sep + 4:].decode("utf-8", errors="replace").strip()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; except ValueError:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pass</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; status, resp = await self._route(method, path, body_str)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; resp_bytes = json.dumps(resp).encode()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; http = (</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"HTTP/1.1 {status}\r\n"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Content-Type: application/json\r\n"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Content-Length: {len(resp_bytes)}\r\n"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"Connection: close\r\n\r\n"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ).encode() + resp_bytes</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writer.write(http)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; await writer.drain()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; except Exception as exc:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; err = json.dumps({"error": str(exc)}).encode()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; http = (f"HTTP/1.1 500 Internal Server Error\r\nContent-Length: {len(err)}\r\n\r\n").encode() + err</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writer.write(http)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; await writer.drain()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; finally:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writer.close()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; async def _route(self, method: str, path: str,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;body: str) -&gt; Tuple[str, Any]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parts = [p for p in path.strip("/").split("/") if p]</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if method == "GET" and parts == ["health"]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return "200 OK", {</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "version": __version__,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "uptime": time.time() - self._start_time,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; "streams": len(self.mss.list_streams()),</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if method == "GET" and parts == ["streams"]:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return "200 OK", {"streams": self.mss.list_streams()}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if method == "GET" and len(parts) == 2 and parts[0] == "status":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return "200 OK", self.mss.status(parts[1])</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if method == "POST" and len(parts) == 2 and parts[0] == "update":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; payload = json.loads(body) if body else {}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; except json.JSONDecodeError:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return "400 Bad Request", {"error": "invalid JSON"}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; value = payload.get("value")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if value is None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return "400 Bad Request", {"error": "missing 'value'"}</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; result = await self.mss.aupdate(parts[1], value)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return "200 OK", result</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if method == "DELETE" and len(parts) == 2 and parts[0] == "stream":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ok = self.mss.delete_stream(parts[1])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return ("200 OK", {"deleted": parts[1]}) if ok else ("404 Not Found", {"error": "not found"})</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if method == "POST" and len(parts) == 2 and parts[0] == "reset":</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ok = self.mss.reset_stream(parts[1])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return ("200 OK", {"reset": parts[1]}) if ok else ("404 Not Found", {"error": "not found"})</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return "404 Not Found", {"error": f"no route for {method} {path}"}</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; async def serve_forever(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Start async server (runs until cancelled)."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._server = await asyncio.start_server(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self._handle, self.host, self.port</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; async with self._server:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; await self._server.serve_forever()</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def run(self) -&gt; None:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; """Blocking entry point (wraps asyncio.run)."""</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; asyncio.run(self.serve_forever())</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; except KeyboardInterrupt:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pass</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># CLI entry point</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div>def _cli_main(argv=None):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prog="fracttalix_sentinel_v800",</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; description="Fracttalix Sentinel v8.0 streaming anomaly detector",</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; )</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser.add_argument("--file", "-f", help="CSV file path (reads first column)")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser.add_argument("--alpha", type=float, default=0.1)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser.add_argument("--multiplier", type=float, default=3.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser.add_argument("--warmup", type=int, default=30)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser.add_argument("--serve", action="store_true", help="Start HTTP server")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser.add_argument("--host", default="0.0.0.0")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser.add_argument("--port", type=int, default=8765)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser.add_argument("--benchmark", action="store_true", help="Run benchmark suite")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser.add_argument("--version", action="version", version=f"%(prog)s {__version__}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; args = parser.parse_args(argv)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; cfg = SentinelConfig(alpha=args.alpha, multiplier=args.multiplier,</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;warmup_periods=args.warmup)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if args.benchmark:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bench = SentinelBenchmark(config=cfg)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bench.run_suite()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if args.serve:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; server = SentinelServer(host=args.host, port=args.port, config=cfg)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(f"Sentinel v{__version__} server on {args.host}:{args.port}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; server.run()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; if args.file:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; det = SentinelDetector(config=cfg)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; with open(args.file, newline="") as f:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; reader = csv.reader(f)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for row in reader:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if not row:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; continue</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; v = float(row[0])</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; except (ValueError, IndexError):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; continue</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; r = det.update_and_check(v)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if r.get("alert"):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(f"[ALERT] step={r['step']} value={v:.4f} "</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f"z={r.get('z_score', 0):.2f} reasons={r.get('alert_reasons', [])}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; parser.print_help()</div><div><br></div><div><br></div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div># 40-test smoke suite</div><div># ===========================================================================</div><div><br></div><div>def _run_tests():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; import traceback</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; passed = 0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; failed = 0</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; errors = []</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def ok(name):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; nonlocal passed</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; passed += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(f" &nbsp;[PASS] {name}")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def fail(name, reason):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; nonlocal failed</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; failed += 1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; errors.append((name, reason))</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; print(f" &nbsp;[FAIL] {name}: {reason}")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def run(name, fn):</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fn()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ok(name)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; except Exception as e:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fail(name, f"{type(e).__name__}: {e}")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; print(f"\n{'='*60}")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; print(f" &nbsp;Fracttalix Sentinel v{__version__} — 65-test Smoke Suite")</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; print(f"{'='*60}\n")</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # T01 — T05: SentinelConfig</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def t01():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cfg = SentinelConfig()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; assert cfg.alpha == 0.1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; assert cfg.warmup_periods == 30</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; run("T01 SentinelConfig defaults", t01)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def t02():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cfg = SentinelConfig(alpha=0.2, multiplier=2.5)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; assert cfg.alpha == 0.2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; assert cfg.multiplier == 2.5</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; run("T02 SentinelConfig custom values", t02)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def t03():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; try:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; SentinelConfig(alpha=0.0)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; assert False, "should raise"</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; except ValueError:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pass</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; run("T03 SentinelConfig validation: alpha=0 raises", t03)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def t04():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cfg1 = SentinelConfig(alpha=0.1)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cfg2 = dataclasses.replace(cfg1, alpha=0.2)</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; assert cfg1.alpha == 0.1</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; assert cfg2.alpha == 0.2</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; run("T04 SentinelConfig replace returns new instance", t04)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; def t05():</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; f = SentinelConfig.fast()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; p = SentinelConfig.production()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; s = SentinelConfig.sensitive()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; r = SentinelConfig.realtime()</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; assert f.alpha &gt; p.alpha</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; assert s.alpha &lt; p.alpha</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; assert r.quantile_threshold_mode</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; run("T05 SentinelConfig factory presets", t05)</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; # ------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div>&nbsp;
